## The Query Path

### 1. HTTP Request Handler (Entry Point)
- `pkg/api/ds_query.go` - `QueryMetricsV2` is the HTTP handler for `POST /ds/query`. It calls `queryDataService.QueryData()` or `QueryDataNew()`.

### 2. Query Service (Core Orchestration)
- `pkg/services/query/query.go` - `ServiceImpl` with `QueryData`, `QueryDataNew`, `queryData`, `handleQuerySingleDatasource`, `handleExpressions`, `executeConcurrentQueries`, `parseMetricRequest`
- `pkg/services/query/models.go` - `parsedQuery`, `parsedRequest` types
- `pkg/services/query/errors.go` - Error types

### 3. Plugin Client (Backend Plugin Dispatch)
- `pkg/plugins/manager/client/client.go` - `Service.QueryData()` - the main plugin client that dispatches to the plugin registry
- `pkg/plugins/ifaces.go` - `Client` interface definition
- `pkg/plugins/plugins.go` - `Plugin.QueryData()` - delegates to the backend plugin client
- `pkg/plugins/backendplugin/ifaces.go` - `Plugin` interface (backend plugin)

### 4. Backend Plugin Implementations
- `pkg/plugins/backendplugin/coreplugin/core_plugin.go` - `corePlugin.QueryData()` - for built-in plugins
- `pkg/plugins/backendplugin/grpcplugin/grpc_plugin.go` - `grpcPlugin.QueryData()` - for external gRPC plugins
- `pkg/plugins/backendplugin/grpcplugin/client_v2.go` - `ClientV2.QueryData()` - actual gRPC call

### 5. Plugin Client Middleware (Instrumentation)
- `pkg/services/pluginsintegration/clientmiddleware/tracing_middleware.go` - `TracingMiddleware.QueryData()`
- `pkg/services/pluginsintegration/clientmiddleware/metrics_middleware.go` - `MetricsMiddleware.QueryData()`
- `pkg/services/pluginsintegration/clientmiddleware/logger_middleware.go

**Summary of what was found:**

The query path flows through these key layers:

1. **HTTP Handler** (`pkg/api/ds_query.go`) — `QueryMetricsV2` receives `POST /ds/query` and calls the query service

3. **Plugin Client Stack** (`pkg/plugins/manager/client/client.go`, `pkg/plugins/plugins.go`) — dispatches to the correct backend plugin via the registry

4. **Backend Plugin Implementations**:
   - Core/in-process: `pkg/plugins/backendplugin/coreplugin/core_plugin.go`
   - External gRPC: `pkg/plugins/backendplugin/grpcplugin/grpc_plugin.go` + `client_v2.go`

5. **Middleware Chain** (14 middlewares in `pkg/services/pluginsintegration/clientmiddleware/`) — tracing, metrics, logging, caching, OAuth, cookies, headers

6. **Expression Service** (`pkg/expr/`) — `TransformData` → `BuildPipeline` → `ExecutePipeline` → `DSNode.Execute` → `ResultConverter.Convert`

7. **New k8s-style APIs**:
   - Unified query: `pkg/registry/apis/query/query.go`

 300  //\n   301  // Based on https://github.com/golang/go/blob/dc04f3ba1f25313bc9c97e728620206c235db9ee/src/net/http/httputil/reverseproxy.go#L411-L421\n   302  func removeConnectionHeaders(h textproto.TrimString(sf); sf != \"\" {\n   306                                  for k := range h {\n   307                                          if textproto.CanonicalMIMEHeaderKey(sf) == textproto.CanonicalMIMEHeaderKey(k) {\n   308                                                  delete(h, k)\n   309                                                  break\n   310                                          }\n   311                                  }\n   312                          }\n   313                  }\n   314          }\n   315  }\n   316\n   317  // Hop-by-hop headers. These are removed when sent to the backend.\n   318  // As of RFC 7230, hop-by-hop headers are required to appear in the\n   319  // Connection header field. These are the headers defined by the\n   320  // obsoleted RFC 2616 (section 13.5.1) and are used for backward\n   321  // compatibility.\n   322  //\n   323  // Copied from https://github.com/golang/go/blob/dc04f3ba1f25313bc9c97e728620206c235db9ee/src/net/http/httputil/reverseproxy.go#L171-L186\n   324  var hopHeaders = []string{\n   325          \"Connection\",\n   326          \"Proxy-Connection\", // non-standard but still sent by libcurl and rejected by e.g. google\n   327          \"Keep-Alive\",\n   328          \"Proxy-Authenticate\",\n   329          \"Proxy-Authorization\",\n   330          \"Te\",      // canonicalized version of \"TE\"\n   331          \"Trailer\", // not Trailers per URL above; https://www.rfc-editor.org/errata_search.php?eid=4522\n   332          \"Transfer-Encoding\",\n   333          \"Upgrade\",\n   334          \"User-Agent\",\n   335  }\n   336\n   337  // removeHopByHopHeaders removes hop-by-hop headers. Especially\n   338  // important is \"Connection\" because we want a persistent\n   339  // connection, regardless of what the client sent to us.\n   340  //\n   341  // Based on https://github.com/golang/go/blob/dc04f3ba1f25313bc9c97e728620206c235db9ee/src/net/http/httputil/reverseproxy.go#L276-L281\n   342  func removeHopByHopHeaders(h map[string][]string) {\n   343          for _, hh := range hopHeaders {\n   344                  for k := range h {\n   345                          if hh == textproto.CanonicalMIMEHeaderKey(k) {\n   346                                  delete(h, k)\n   347                                  break\n   348                          }\n   349                  }\n   350          }\n   351  }\n   352\n   353  func removeNonAllowedHeaders(h map[string][]string) {\n   354          for k := range h {\n   355                  if textproto.CanonicalMIMEHeaderKey(k) == setCookieHeaderName {\n   356                          delete(h, k)\n   357                  }\n   358          }\n   359  }\n   360\n   361  // ensureContentTypeHeader makes sure a content type always is returned in response.\n   362  func ensureContentTypeHeader(res *backend.CallResourceResponse) {\n   363          if res == nil {\n   364                  return\n   365          }\n   366\n   367          var hasContentType bool\n   368          for k := range res.Headers {\n   369                  if textproto.CanonicalMIMEHeaderKey(k) == contentTypeHeaderName {\n   370                          hasContentType = true\n   371                          break\n   372                  }\n   373          }\n   374\n   375          if !hasContentType && res.Status != http.StatusNoContent {\n   376                  res.Headers[contentTypeHeaderName] = []string{defaultContentType}\n   377          }\n   378  }"

grafana/grafana.\\n\\n## 1. HTTP Request Handler (Entry Point)\\n\\n**`pkg/api/ds_query.go`** is the primary HTTP entry point. `QueryMetricsV2` handles `POST /ds/query` requests. It binds the incoming JSON body to a `dtos.MetricRequest`, then calls `queryDataService.QueryData()` or `QueryDataNew()` (the latter supports per-query time ranges). The `getDSQueryEndpoint()` function optionally rewrites requests to the new Kubernetes-style query API (`/apis/query.grafana.app/v0alpha1/...`) when the `queryServiceRewrite` feature flag is enabled. The `toJsonStreamingResponse()` function transforms the `backend.QueryDataResponse` into a streaming JSON HTTP response.\\n\\n**`pkg/api/dtos/models.go`** defines `MetricRequest`, the DTO for incoming query requests containing `From`, `To`, and `Queries` fields.\\n\\n## 2. Query Service (Core Orchestration)\\n\\n**`pkg/services/query/query.go`** is the heart of the query path. `ServiceImpl` implements the `Service` interface with:\\n- `queryData()` \u2014 parses the request, then routes to `handleExpressions()`, `handleQuerySingleDatasource()`, or `executeConcurrentQueries()` depending on whether expressions are present and how many datasources are involved.\\n- `parseMetricRequest()` \u2014 parses the raw JSON queries, resolves datasource references, and builds `parsedRequest` with per-datasource query groups.\\n- `handleQuerySingleDatasource()` \u2014 builds a `backend.QueryDataRequest` and dispatches it to `pluginClient.QueryData()` (single-tenant) or `qsDsClient.QueryData()` (multi-tenant/query-service flow).\\n- `executeConcurrentQueries()` \u2014 fans out queries to multiple datasources concurrently using `errgroup`.\\n- `handleExpressions()` \u2014 delegates to `expr.Service.TransformData()` for expression queries.\\n\\n**`pkg/services/query/models.go`** defines `parsedQuery` and `parsedRequest` types used internally.\\n\\n**`pkg/services/query/errors.go`** defines typed errors like `ErrNoQueriesFound`, `ErrInvalidDatasourceID`, `ErrDuplicateRefId`.\\n\\n## 3. Plugin Client Interface and Dispatch\\n\\n**`pkg/plugins/ifaces.go`** defines the `Client` interface (which embeds `backend.Handler`) \u2014 the top-level interface for communicating with backend plugins.\\n\\n**`pkg/plugins/manager/client/client.go`** provides `Service`, the concrete implementation of `plugins.Client`. Its `QueryData()` method looks up the plugin from the registry and delegates to `plugin.QueryData()`.\\n\\n**`pkg/plugins/plugins.go`** defines the `Plugin` struct. Its `QueryData()` method delegates to the underlying `backendplugin.Plugin` client registered via `RegisterClient()`.\\n\\n**`pkg/plugins/backendplugin/ifaces.go`** defines the `backendplugin.Plugin` interface, which embeds `backend.QueryDataHandler` among other handlers.\\n\\n## 4. Backend Plugin Implementations\\n\\n**`pkg/plugins/backendplugin/coreplugin/core_plugin.go`** \u2014 `corePlugin.QueryData()` handles built-in (in-process) plugins by calling the registered `backend.QueryDataHandler`.\\n\\n**`pkg/plugins/backendplugin/coreplugin/registry.go`** \u2014 `Registry` and `ProvideCoreRegistry()` register all core datasource plugins (Prometheus, Loki, CloudWatch, etc.) as `backendplugin.PluginFactoryFunc` instances.\\n\\n**`pkg/plugins/backendplugin/grpcplugin/grpc_plugin.go`** \u2014 `grpcPlugin.QueryData()` handles external gRPC plugins by delegating to `ClientV2.QueryData()`.\\n\\n**`pkg/plugins/backendplugin/grpcplugin/client_v2.go`** \u2014 `ClientV2.QueryData()` performs the actual gRPC call: it serializes the request via `backend.ToProto().QueryDataRequest()`, calls `DataClient.QueryData()` over gRPC, and deserializes the response via `backend.FromProto().QueryDataResponse()`.\\n\\n**`pkg/plugins/backendplugin/grpcplugin/client_proto.go`** \u2014 defines `ProtoClient` and `protoClient` for the gRPC protocol layer.\\n\\n## 5. Plugin Client Middleware (Instrumentation Layer)\\n\\n**`pkg/services/pluginsintegration/pluginsintegration.go`** \u2014 `CreateMiddlewares()` assembles the middleware chain; `NewMiddlewareHandler()` wraps the base `client.Service` with all middlewares using `backend.HandlerFromMiddlewares()`.\\n\\nThe middleware chain (in order) includes:\\n- **`tracing_middleware.go`** (`TracingMiddleware`) \u2014 creates OpenTelemetry spans per request.\\n- **`metrics_middleware.go`** (`MetricsMiddleware`) \u2014 records Prometheus metrics (request count, duration, size).\\n- **`contextual_logger_middleware.go`** (`ContextualLoggerMiddleware`) \u2014 adds contextual logger to context.\\n- **`logger_middleware.go`** (`LoggerMiddleware`) \u2014 logs plugin requests and responses.\\n- **`tracing_header_middleware.go`** (`TracingHeaderMiddleware`) \u2014 propagates tracing headers (X-Datasource-Uid, X-Dashboard-Uid, etc.).\\n- **`clear_auth_headers_middleware.go`** (`ClearAuthHeadersMiddleware`) \u2014 strips Grafana auth headers from outgoing requests.\\n- **`oauthtoken_middleware.go`** (`OAuthTokenMiddleware`) \u2014 forwards OAuth tokens when `oauthPassThru` is enabled.\\n- **`cookies_middleware.go`** (`CookiesMiddleware`) \u2014 forwards cookies when `keepCookies` is configured.\\n- **`caching_middleware.go`** (`CachingMiddleware`) \u2014 implements query result caching.\\n- **`forward_id_middleware.go`** (`ForwardIDMiddleware`) \u2014 sets `X-Grafana-Id` header.\\n- **`usealertingheaders_middleware.go`** (`UseAlertHeadersMiddleware`) \u2014 applies alerting-specific headers.\\n- **`user_header_middleware.go`** (`UserHeaderMiddleware`) \u2014 sets `X-Grafana-User` header.\\n- **`grafana_request_id_header_middleware.go`** (`HostedGrafanaACHeaderMiddleware`) \u2014 sets signed request ID for IP range access control.\\n- **`httpclient_middleware.go`** (`HTTPClientMiddleware`) \u2014 forwards plugin request headers as HTTP headers.\\n\\n## 6. Expression Service (Server-Side Expressions)\\n\\n**`pkg/expr/transform.go`** \u2014 `Service.TransformData()` is the main entry point for expression queries. It calls `BuildPipeline()` then `ExecutePipeline()`.\\n\\n**`pkg/expr/service.go`** \u2014 `Service.BuildPipeline()` and `Service.ExecutePipeline()` orchestrate the expression pipeline.\\n\\n**`pkg/expr/graph.go`** \u2014 `Service.buildPipeline()` constructs a DAG of expression and datasource nodes; `DataPipeline.execute()` runs them in topological order.\\n\\n**`pkg/expr/nodes.go`** \u2014 `DSNode.Execute()` executes individual datasource queries within the expression pipeline, dispatching to either the single-tenant plugin client or the multi-tenant query-service client.\\n\\n**`pkg/expr/query_convert.go`** \u2014 `ConvertBackendRequestToDataRequest()` converts `backend.QueryDataRequest` to the k8s-style `data.QueryDataRequest` for the query-service flow.\\n\\n**`pkg/expr/converter.go`** \u2014 `ResultConverter.Convert()` transforms datasource response frames into `mathexp.Results` for use in expression evaluation.\\n\\n**`pkg/expr/errors.go`** \u2014 defines expression-specific error types (`MakeQueryError`, `makeConversionError`, etc.).\\n\\n## 7. New Kubernetes-Style Query API\\n\\n**`pkg/registry/apis/query/query.go`** \u2014 `queryREST.Connect()` handles `POST /apis/query.grafana.app/v0alpha1/namespaces/{ns}/query`. The `handleQuery()` function converts the k8s-style request back to a `dtos.MetricRequest` and calls `service.QueryData()`.\\n\\n**`pkg/registry/apis/query/register.go`** \u2014 `QueryAPIBuilder` and `RegisterAPIService()` register the query API group with the Grafana API server.\\n\\n**`pkg/registry/apis/query/header_utils.go`** \u2014 `ExtractKnownHeaders()` extracts known forwarding headers from HTTP requests.\\n\\n**`pkg/registry/apis/query/client/plugin.go`** \u2014 `pluginClient.QueryData()` implements `QueryDataClient` for the single-tenant flow, performing access control checks and delegating to `plugins.Client.QueryData()`.\\n\\n**`pkg/registry/apis/query/client/instance_provider.go`** \u2014 `singleTenantInstanceProvider` provides `Instance` objects for single-tenant deployments.\\n\\n**`pkg/registry/apis/query/clientapi/clientapi.go`** \u2014 defines `QueryDataClient`, `Instance`, and `InstanceProvider` interfaces used by the query API.\\n\\n## 8. Per-Datasource API (Datasource API Servers)\\n\\n**`pkg/registry/apis/datasource/sub_query.go`** \u2014 `subQueryREST.Connect()` handles `POST /apis/{group}/v0alpha1/namespaces/{ns}/datasources/{uid}/query` for individual datasource API servers.\\n\\n**`pkg/registry/apis/datasource/register.go`** \u2014 `DataSourceAPIBuilder` and `RegisterAPIService()` register per-datasource API groups. Defines the `PluginClient` interface subset used by datasource APIs.\\n\\n**`pkg/registry/apis/datasource/querier.go`** \u2014 `DefaultQuerier.Query()` wraps `plugins.Client.QueryData()` with namespace validation.\\n\\n**`pkg/registry/apis/datasource/queryconvert.go`** \u2014 `queryConvertREST` handles query schema conversion requests.\\n\\n**`pkg/registry/apis/datasource/plugincontext.go`** \u2014 `PluginDatasourceProvider` and `PluginContextWrapper` interfaces; `scopedDatasourceProvider` provides datasource instance settings.\\n\\n**`pkg/registry/apis/datasource/middleware.go`** \u2014 `contextualMiddlewares()` applies HTTP client middlewares (response limit, SigV4) based on plugin context.\\n\\n## 9. Aggregator Plugin Handler\\n\\n**`pkg/aggregator/apiserver/plugin/handler.go`** \u2014 `PluginHandler` routes requests to registered plugin services.\\n\\n**`pkg/aggregator/apiserver/plugin/query.go`** \u2014 `PluginHandler.QueryDataHandler()` handles query requests for aggregated datasource API servers, validating datasource UID/type and calling `client.QueryData()`.\\n\\n## 10. Response Types\\n\\n**`pkg/apis/query/v0alpha1/query.go`** \u2014 defines `QueryDataRequest` and `QueryDataResponse` (k8s runtime.Object wrappers around the SDK types), and `GetResponseCode()` for determining HTTP status from query responses.\\n\\n## 11. Plugin Context\\n\\n**`pkg/services/pluginsintegration/plugincontext/plugincontext.go`** \u2014 `Provider.GetWithDataSource()` builds the `backend.PluginContext` for datasource queries, including decrypted datasource settings.\\n\\n**`pkg/services/pluginsintegration/plugincontext/base_plugincontext.go`** \u2014 `BaseProvider.GetBasePluginContext()` builds the base plugin context with user, org, and Grafana config.\\n\\n**`pkg/services/pluginsintegration/adapters/adapters.go`** \u2014 `ModelToInstanceSettings()` converts `datasources.DataSource` to `backend.DataSourceInstanceSettings`.\\n\\n## 12.
